CIDC Data Model

CYTOF Run

Description: Information about the acquisition and analysis CyTOF data.

Properties

Property Description Data Type
Inherits all properties from schema: assays.cytof_assay_core
assay_creator
required 		Indicates what site is filling out the assay. assays.components.assay_core#assay_creator
assay_run_id
required 		User defined unique identifier for this assay run. Not necessarily unique across batches. assays.cytof_assay_core#assay_run_id
cytof_antibodies
required 		assays.cytof_assay_core#cytof_antibodies
batch_id
required 		CyTOF batch identification number. Unique to every batch. assays.cytof_assay_core#batch_id
records
required 		A single sample-level data record from CyTOF a assay batch. < array >
assays.cytof_assay_core#entry
barcodes assays.cytof_assay_core#barcodes
controls assays.cytof_assay_core#controls
excluded_samples assays.cytof_assay_core#excluded_samples
injector Name of Injector component used as part of the CyTOF software < string >
date_of_acquisition Date of CyTOF batch acquisition. < string >
bead_removal Boolean to indicate whether beads have been removed after normalization process < boolean >
acquisition_buffer Cell staining buffer used for antibody and cell dilution. < string >
instrument Name of CyTOF instrument on which experiment was conducted. < string >
normalization_method Process used for normalization prior to analysis, if any. < string >
  • "Fluidigm"
  • "Normalizer v0.3"
  • "Other"
debarcoding_protocol The strategy/kit used to barcode CyTOF samples, if any < string >
harware_version Version no. of instrument hardware used. < string >
source_fcs < array >
artifacts.artifact_fcs
barcoding_key_csv Information about a comma separated file. artifacts.artifact_csv
astrolabe_reports Information about a ZIP file. artifacts.artifact_zip
astrolabe_analysis Information about a ZIP file. artifacts.artifact_zip
control_files_analysis Information about a ZIP file. artifacts.artifact_zip

{
    "$id": "cytof_assay",
    "$schema": "metaschema/strict_meta_schema.json#",

                        },

                        },

                        },

                            "description": "Antibody isotype used to help differentiate antibody signals.",

                        },

                            "description": "Identification number assigned to the particular quantity or lot of material from manufacturer.",
                            "type": "string"
                        },

                                "Surface Stain",
                                "Intracellular"
                            ],
